| <span data-ttu-id="8e592-707">Entrada</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e592-707">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="8e592-708">Valor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8e592-708">Value</span></span> |
